###1939-41 tech: game_balance_tech_stage_1b
game_balance_tech_stage_1b = {
allow = {
 has_country_flag = impossible
 OR = {
 AND = {
  date = 1939.1.1
  game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 0
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 1 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1939.4.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 1
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 2 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1939.8.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 2
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 3 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1939.12.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 3
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 4 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1940.4.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 4
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 5 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1940.8.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 5
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 6 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1940.12.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 6
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 7 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1941.4.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 7
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 8 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1941.8.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 8
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 9 }
 }
 }
}

###1942-44 tech: game_balance_tech_stage_2
game_balance_tech_stage_2 = {
allow = {
 has_country_flag = impossible
 OR = {
 AND = {
  date = 1942.4.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 1
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 2 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1942.8.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 2
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 3 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1942.12.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 3
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 4 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1943.4.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 4
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 5 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1943.8.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 5
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 6 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1943.12.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 6
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 7 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1944.4.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 7
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 8 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1944.8.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 8
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_2 = 9 }
 }
 }
}

allow = {
 has_country_flag = impossible
 OR = {

  game_balance_tech_stage_3 = 1
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_3 = 2 }
 }

  date = 1945.8.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_3 = 2
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_3 = 3 }
 }

  date = 1945.12.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_3 = 3
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_3 = 4 }
 }

  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_3 = 5 }
 }
